	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　羽入はそっと手を開き、…それを見た。",
		   NULL, "Hanyuu slowly opened her hand and looked at it.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　それは、",
		   NULL, "It was...", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "………鷹野の放った弾丸。",
		   NULL, " the bullet Takano had fired.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　奇跡の起こったことの、証。",
		   NULL, "This was the proof of their miracle.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　羽入がここにいていいことの証。",
		   NULL, "It was the proof that Hanyuu could exist there.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode) == 0) { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　そして、……いつまでもいつまでも一緒にいていいのだという、…証…。",
		   NULL, "It was the proof that they could be together, forever and ever...", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DrawScene( "background/hi1", 400 );
	ModFadeOutBGM( 0, 400, FALSE, 1 );

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#6972c1>梨花</color>", NULL, "<color=#6972c1>Rika</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 5, "ps3/s13/05/ds41050554", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「もうすぐ、暗くなってお祭りの時間になりますです。」",
		   NULL, "\"It'll be dark soon. It's time for the festival.\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#8676cf>羽入</color>", NULL, "<color=#8676cf>Hanyuu</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 12, "ps3/s13/12/ds41070443", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「……あぅ。」",
		   NULL, "\"...Au.\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#6972c1>梨花</color>", NULL, "<color=#6972c1>Rika</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 5, "ps3/s13/05/ds41050555", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「みんなで楽しくお祭りで部活なのです。",
		   NULL, "\"We'll have so much fun together.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 5, "ps3/s13/05/ds41050556", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "もう脇で見てることなんかできませんです。",
		   NULL, " You can't just watch us anymore.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 5, "ps3/s13/05/ds41050557", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "きっと新人イジメの洗礼で罰ゲーム三昧でかぁいそかぁいそなのです。」",
		   NULL, " I'm sure there will be plenty of punishments to torment the poor, poor newcomer.\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#8676cf>羽入</color>", NULL, "<color=#8676cf>Hanyuu</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 12, "ps3/s13/12/ds41070444", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「………もう、綿流しのお祭り、見てるだけじゃないのですね。」",
		   NULL, "\"......I don't have to just watch the Watanagashi festival, huh?\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#6972c1>梨花</color>", NULL, "<color=#6972c1>Rika</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 5, "ps3/s13/05/ds41050558", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「そうです。だってお祭りは、見るものじゃなくて、加わるものですよ。」",
		   NULL, "\"That's right. Because you don't watch a festival... you enjoy it.\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DrawScene( "black", 1000 );
	FadeOutBGM( 1, 1000, TRUE );
}
